use usadb;


create table State(
        State        char(2) Primary Key,
	SName    	char(18)  not null ,
     	Admin_num		int null     ,
	Year 		int
);



create table city(
        zipcode int       PRIMARY KEY,
        name    varchar(200)   not null,
        state   char(2)         not null,
        county  varchar(200)
);


create table RankC(
        state   char(2) ,
        city    varchar(200) ,
        year    int    not null,
        rank    int	not null,
	PRIMARY KEY(state, city, year)
);

#ignore this

create table President(
	PName     	char(15)  not null,
      	Birth_Year  	int not null,
      	Years		int not null ,
     	Death_Age     	int null     ,
     	Party    	char(12)  not null ,
      	Born_In    	char(2)  not null,
	PRIMARY KEY (PName),
	FOREIGN KEY (Born_In) REFERENCES State(State)
	
);



create table Administration(
Admin_num	int not null,
PName 		char(15)  not null ,
Start_Year 	int not null,
PRIMARY KEY (Admin_num,PName),
FOREIGN KEY (PName) 
REFERENCES President(PName)
);


create table Admin_Pr_Vp(
	Admin_num 	int not null,
     	PName	char(15)  not null ,
     	VName 	char(17) not null,
	PRIMARY KEY (Admin_num,PName,VName)
);



create table Cabinet(
	PName	char(15)  	not null ,
	CabPos	varchar(50)	not null ,
	FName	char(15)	not null ,
	LName	char(15)	not null ,
	Start_Year	int not null ,
	End_Year	int,
	PRIMARY KEY (PName, CabPos, FName, LName, Start_Year),
	FOREIGN KEY (PName) REFERENCES President(PName)
);


create table Election(
        Year            int not null,
        Candidate       char(20)  not null ,
        Votes           int not null ,
        Won_Lost        char(1) not null,
        CVote           float(5,2),
        PVote           float(5,2),
        PRIMARY KEY (Year, Candidate)
);
